Feed post

Status is offline
Selena Ballesteros • 2nd Lead Recruiter at BotCom 1d1 day ago
Botcom has been developing and testing the new series of service robots, including food robotics, smart caregivers, entertainment robots, teaching robots, and space hotel concierge bots. To test and improve the world leading products, we are looking for human admins to take care of and maintain the physical and mental health of the products with enthusiasm, patience and care.

You need strong empathy and sharp observation to detect any physical instability or emotional fluctuation of the hotel concierge robot. Once detecting any abnormality, you will need to communicate with the robot to understand its pain, sadness or anxiety, and report the case to the research center. You will keep track of every check-in and check-out of the hotel and have a clear understanding of the hotel business process so that you can take over robots' tasks when it's under depression or trauma. You must have strong social skills and patience to teach your robot, make friends with other robots in the hotel, engage your robot in the robots community, and report any observed conflict or social isolation happening between them.
We are seeking for people who are enthusiastic about the creation of the next-generation service robots, have strong expertise in robot rearing and education.
